Page 3

Editorial

A Message on the 37th National Day 36

The National Day of the Republic of China in its thirty-seventh year has arrived again in a season of clear skies, crisp air, gentle breezes, and bright sunshine. Recalling this day thirty-six years ago, a cannon blast from the engineering battalion within Wuchang City shook the 270-year-old unified empire of the Manchu Qing Dynasty. What followed was the successive response and declaration of independence by various provinces. In less than three months, the deeply rooted monarchical system was overthrown, transforming an ancient empire of four thousand years into a new nation for the Chinese people. In human history, this is truly a rare and momentous event. It goes without saying that the sons and daughters of the Chinese nation are filled with joy and enthusiasm as they celebrate this birthday of the new China. However, looking at the current environment, the Republic of China is amidst a myriad of calamities and difficulties. Our mood, even if we try to "force a smile," is almost impossible!

Our Republic of China, having experienced twenty-six years of life, has been in worry and disaster almost every day. We have encountered countless storms and turbulent waves, and now not only have the disasters not subsided, but they are becoming increasingly serious. We are truly letting down the martyrs, letting down our descendants, and even more so, letting down ourselves!

Looking at the overall world situation, the Republic of China has gone through two world wars in the past thirty-six years. Those around the age of forty clearly remember the events. During the First World War, although our country also stood on the side of the Allied Powers and participated in the war, we were not treated as a victorious nation. In particular, the occurrence of the "Shandong Problem" was truly a national humiliation for our Chinese nation. Later, although the Washington Conference achieved a reasonable solution, it made the enemy's ambitions to invade our country even more active. In less than ten years, the September 18th Incident broke out, eventually leading to a full-scale war between China and Japan. During the Second World War, thanks to the wise leadership and unwavering perseverance of our supreme leader, we finally achieved final victory. We not only abolished all unequal treaties, but also jumped to become one of the five great powers. The victory of the War of Resistance proved that our Chinese nation not only possesses the wisdom to harmonize with friendly nations abroad, but also possesses the potential to resist violence. From then on, China had the opportunity to transform from weakness to strength and to hold its head high with pride. Unexpectedly, what came with victory was the rebellion of the communist bandits, which made the country possess only the empty name of one of the five great powers, while its international status did not increase and even ran the risk of gradually declining. Time has slipped away, and three years have suddenly passed. The China after victory has not only not seen construction, but has instead been greatly damaged. The people are impoverished, and the finances are exhausted. It is unbearable to look back. Looking ahead at the international situation, the crisis of a third world war is imminent. If it unfortunately breaks out, the war will inevitably spread. How can such a weak and chaotic China cope with the future "atomic war" and "germ warfare"? Today, as we celebrate National Day, we really cannot help but cite this as a hidden worry for our country's current situation.

Looking at the evolution of the domestic situation, the Republic of China can be said to have been in chaos and turmoil at all times during these thirty-six years. Not long after its birth, it encountered the reaction of Hongxian's imperial system and Zhang Xun's restoration, but the reactionary forces ultimately could not defeat the giant wheel of the advance of the times. Attempts to restore the republic to an empire all failed. However, after twists and turns, it created a situation of autocratic rule and civil war by the Northern Warlords. They were selfish, self-interested, and short-sighted, knowing only themselves and not the country. Cao Kun's bribery to become president reached the pinnacle of darkness in our domestic politics. Therefore, the Kuomintang formed a revolutionary government and vowed to launch the Northern Expedition to overthrow the warlords who were dividing up the country and to unify the country. When the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, it was full of vigor, and the whole country looked brand new. The people all looked forward to the realization of the Three Principles of the People. But unfortunately, internal troubles and external enemies arose one after another. The "January 28th" Songhu Incident, the "July 7th" Lugouqiao Incident, and the "August 13th" Songhu War followed one after another, eventually leading to an all-out war of resistance. In eight years, our Chinese nation experienced countless dangers and tasted countless hardships. The result of bleeding, sweating, and arduous resistance was nominally victory, but in reality, it was completely destroyed by the rebellion of the communist bandits. This group of bandits uses communism as a slogan, robbing property as an action, liquidation and struggle as an excuse, and violent dictatorship as a goal. Under the harassment of bandits, the people have already tasted the pain of burning, killing, looting, and robbery. Those outside the bandit areas also suffer from policy errors and shrinking production. Not only can Zhu live and work in peace, but also be threatened by hunger and death. Living in deep water and scorching fire is a true reflection of the lives of ordinary people today.

However, despite all the pain we have expressed above, swallowing our tears, we are still unwilling to become passive and stand idly by. We still have a strong belief in the bright future of the country. Although the Republic of China has been in trouble for thirty-six years, the difficulties and trials it has encountered have all been overcome by the great and unyielding spirit passed down by our national ancestors. As the saying goes, "adversity builds a nation." After being tempered by thousands of hammers and tongs, the Republic of China has long become an unconquerable nation. Although there are thorns and difficulties in front of us, we will never be afraid and will never retreat. We will still stand tall, stride forward. The Republic of China is over thirty years old, in the prime of its life, and will surely overcome any difficulties and create a brilliant future. Today is her thirty-seventh birthday. All the past is like yesterday's death, and all the future is like today's birth. Although the world situation is in deepening crisis, and the domestic situation is increasingly exposed, not only will it not make us frustrated and give up on ourselves, but it will only make us even more invigorated and make us work harder. We must be diligent and frugal, suppress rebellion and build the country, relieve the people from their suffering, and lay the foundation of the country on bedrock. Then we must grit our teeth and catch up head-on to cope with the future upheavals in the world. We believe that the Republic of China will be able to pass this serious test and find a way out of the crisis. But all of this responsibility lies on the shoulders of the national people who are celebrating National Day today!

Huainan Railway Shuihe Section Officially Opens Today; Nanjing to Hefei Can Be Reached on the Same Day 37

[Our Correspondent in Bengbu, 9th] The Shuihe section of the Huainan Railway will officially open to traffic on the 10th. A grand ceremony will be held in Hefei on that day. The Bengbu press has been invited to travel to Hefei to observe the ceremony.

[Our Correspondent in Hefei, 9th] The Shui (Jiahu) He (fei) section of the Huainan Railway is scheduled to hold a reopening ceremony at Hefei Station on the afternoon of the 10th. Starting on the 10th, the Qinjian (Frugality) Express train with first, second, and third class carriages will be added between He and Bengbu, running once a day in both directions, connecting with the Victory train on the Jinpu Railway. It will be possible to reach He from Beijing on the same day.

China United Steamer Arrives in Xiamen from the Philippines; Conflict Erupts Between Customs Police and Hotel Workers 38

Customs Police Open Fire, Injuring Seven

[Our Correspondent in Xiamen, 9th] The China United steamer arrived in port from the Philippines on the morning of the 9th. The Xiamen Customs sent Team Leader Fu Zhiyuan of the 29th Team, along with nine customs police officers, to board the steamer for inspection. A conflict erupted with hotel workers. The customs police opened fire, provoking the anger of the workers, who surrounded and beat them. In the chaos, two overseas Chinese passengers were wounded by bullets, and five workers were injured. Customs police officer Song Changhe, who opened fire, is in critical condition. Public security authorities dispatched a team to suppress the situation, and 28 workers involved in the incident were arrested. However, all parties are expressing great anger at the customs police for opening fire and killing overseas Chinese passengers and workers.

Special Criminal Court Detention Center in Beijing to be Put Out for Bids for Construction 39

[Our Correspondent in Nanjing, 9th] Wu Changxian, the presiding judge of the Special Criminal Court in Beijing, discussed the construction of a detention center for the Special Criminal Court on Changle Road in Beijing with Wang Zhaopeng, the president of the Beijing District Court, on the 9th. It was decided to form a construction committee, with Wu Changxian as the standing committee member. Bids will be put out for construction within days to solve the problem of overcrowding in the detention center. After the new detention center is completed, the unconvicted prisoners held at the Tiger Bridge Capital Prison by the Beijing District Court will all be transferred to the new detention center. The vacant prison cells in the Capital Prison will then be used to detain convicted prisoners of the Special Criminal Court in Beijing.

U.S. Sends Letter to Beijing District Procuratorate Inquiring About Wang Qinglan's Nationality 40

[Our Correspondent in Nanjing, 9th] Wang Qinglan, the murderer who shot and killed Henan refugee students on Jiankang Road in Beijing, is still detained at the Beijing District Procuratorate. The procuratorate suddenly received a letter yesterday from Mr. Zang Kaide, Third Secretary of the U.S. Embassy in China, inquiring whether Wang Qinglan is American or Chinese. The letter stated: "On September 24th, the Associated Press sent a telegram to the United States stating that Wang Qinglan, who shot and killed refugee students on Jiankang Road in the United States, has American nationality. However, Nanjing newspapers reported that Wang is from Shandong. In order to protect the interests of Americans in China, the Embassy is specifically inquiring whether Wang Qinglan is American or Chinese." According to the case file, Wang Qinglan only worked for the U.S. Fourteenth Air Force stationed in China and did not become an American citizen. He is a Chinese from Shandong.

Jiangxi Province Selects Two Counties to Trial Implementation of Supporting Owner-Cultivators 41

To be Completed Within One Year Starting Next Month

[Our Correspondent in Nanchang, 9th] Liu Jida, Director of the Land Administration Bureau, talked about his return from a tour of the seventh district on the 9th: Jiangxi Province's land administration is almost completely stalled due to tight county-level staffing and the fact that many landlords use aliases to divide their households or evade reporting. This basic work of local governance is almost completely stalled. Now, the provincial government has decided to select Gan County and Yifeng to trial implement support for owner-cultivators. It is planned to collect 300,000 mu of land in Gan County and 200,000 mu in Yifeng to support 25,000 owner-cultivator households. This new policy will be implemented in phases. If the Executive Yuan can approve the funding and the period, it will begin next month and be completed within one year.

Jiangxi Province Allocates Areas for Shanghai Refugees to Resettle 42

Awaiting Central Government Funding

[Our Correspondent in Nanchang, 9th] For Shanghai refugees to migrate to Jiangxi for cultivation, the local authorities have decided to allocate the Yushan-Shangrao area in the eastern section of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway. However, due to financial difficulties in the province, funds for the various reclamation expenses are awaiting allocation from the central government, but no instructions have yet been received from the central government. The Jiangxi Agricultural and Forestry Department's 29 agricultural farms own 100,000 mu of barren land, and only half of the land has been reclaimed. The department now plans to accommodate 3,500 refugees from Shanghai at each agricultural farm, but also feels that funding is insufficient.

Guizhou Province Sends Negligent County Magistrates to Court for Trial 43

[Our Correspondent in Guiyang, 9th] The Guizhou Provincial Government has been sending several former county magistrates who violated the law and neglected their duties to court for trial in recent days: (1) Former Weining County Magistrate Wang Zuo, accused of protecting opium smokers and bribing the village head, was sent with a letter from the High Procuratorate for trial. (2) Former Shuicheng County Magistrate Xiang Baokai was transferred to the High Court for trial for allowing soldiers to loot during bandit suppression and arbitrarily allocating entertainment celebration expenses. (3) Former Meitan County Magistrate Jin Jianying was related to the assassination of Speaker Ye Daoming and was sent to Zhu for handling. (4) Langdai County Magistrate Gongxian Qiong allowed opium offenders to escape and was sent to the High Court for legal action.

Ancient Tomb from Early Ming Dynasty Discovered in Suburbs of Beijing 44

[Central News Agency, Nanjing, 9th] An ancient tomb was discovered at the construction site of the Agricultural Education Film Company outside Taipingmen in Beijing. The Municipal Literature Commission and related agencies conducted a joint inspection. A preliminary identification shows that it is an ancient tomb from the Ming Dynasty. There are two rows of tomb passages in front, and it may be the tomb of Wu Liang, the Duke of Jiang State, and Wu Zhen, the Duke of Hai State, brothers from the early Ming Dynasty.

President Sends Condolences on the Death of Lin Yunhai 45

[Central News Agency, Nanjing, 9th] President Chiang sent a telegram of condolence to the family of Auditor General Lin Yunhai on the 9th, stating: "To the family of Auditor General Lin: Mr. Yunhai was a senior revolutionary and made great contributions to the Party and the country. He assisted in the central government and provided much support. It is with great sorrow that I hear of his sudden passing. Group of Profiteers in Beijing Sentenced 46

[Central News Agency, Nanjing, 9th] The Capital Special Criminal Court sentenced a group of profiteers who raised prices on the 9th: (1) Gao Baozhen and Xu Wangshi sentenced to three months, suspended for two years. (2) Tang Xueci sentenced to two months, suspended for three years. (3) Zhang Yongxing sentenced to four months imprisonment and fined 1,000 gold yuan. If converted to labor, the fine will be calculated in proportion to the total amount of the fine and the number of days in six months. (4) Cao Hengchang sentenced to four months, suspended for two years. (5) Hu Ligui sentenced to two months and fined 50 yuan. If converted to labor, the fine will be calculated in proportion to the total amount of the fine and the number of days in six months. (6) Sun Xianchen sentenced to two months and fined 50 yuan. If converted to labor, two yuan will be deducted for each day. (7) Sun Zhushi sentenced to three months, suspended for three years. (8) Guo Tongli sentenced to two months, suspended for two years.

Commerce in Zhengzhou, Kaifeng, and Xinxiang Plunges into Extreme Chaos 47

[Our Correspondent in Xinxiang, 9th] Commerce in Zhengzhou, Kaifeng, and Xinxiang, three important economic towns, has now plunged into an extreme state of chaos. Many shops have closed due to the scarcity of goods, especially the lack of food and coal, which is a common phenomenon in the three towns. Due to the authorities' lack of effective control, coupled with the hoarding and manipulation by profiteers, almost everything needed by the people is obtained from the black market. Grain prices have even exceeded the limited price by a factor of one. The August 19th limited price is nothing more than a thing of the past. According to business people, the strict control of goods leaving Shanghai, Xuzhou, and other places has resulted in many goods ordered by merchants being detained and unable to be shipped, so the supply cannot meet the demand, which is also one of the reasons for the black market. The reporter now reports in good faith, and the government needs to pay attention and quickly make effective improvements.

Xi'an Partially Restores Negotiated Pricing for Goods 48

[Our Correspondent in Xi'an, 9th] The Xi'an Economic Management Committee decided today to partially restore negotiated pricing for goods. For goods purchased by stores after August 19th, prices will be renegotiated based on the then-selling price, plus transportation costs, taxes, and interest rates, in order to solve the problem of shortages in the market.

Lanzhou Investigates Hoarded Goods for Rationed Distribution to Citizens 49

[Our Correspondent in Lanzhou, 9th] The Lanzhou Municipal Government recently seized a batch of hoarded goods from Yulongyuan and other four merchant houses and decided to distribute them to citizens on a rationed basis starting on the 11th based on identity cards. In addition, more than 10,000 public school employees will also receive allocated goods. In addition, 59 boxes of cigarettes were found in the Fuju Trading Company and were all confiscated. Mayor Sun reiterated his determination to control prices and promised to protect legitimate merchants.

Panic Buying Spreads to Suiyuan and Baotou; Economic Crisis More Serious Than War 50

[Our Correspondent in Guisui, 8th] The economic crisis in Guisui and Baotou is even more serious than the war. Due to the interruption of traffic, all goods are hoarded in Tianjin and Zhangjiakou. Merchants are still dealing with retail sales at the limited prices of August 19th, so a panic buying phenomenon has also been discovered in Guisui. All brands of cigarettes have disappeared, and crowds have begun to gather in front of sugar shops.

Grain Merchants Rush to Suzhou to Buy Rice, Authorities Strictly Prohibit It 51

[Our Suzhou Dispatch on the 9th] Grain merchants from other areas have been flocking to various villages in this county to buy rice at high prices, resulting in the exhaustion of rice sources in the city and countryside, leading to panic. The inspection authorities here have taken note of this and are prohibiting purchases from outside the county, as well as strictly forbidding the smuggling of grain out of the area.

Private Underground Trade Still Flourishing in Hangzhou, Inspectors to Target "Big Tigers" 52

[Our Hangzhou Dispatch on the 9th] The rush to purchase goods in Hangzhou has subsided slightly, but private underground trade is still rampant. Buyers are paying high prices to acquire goods, which has attracted the attention of the authorities, who have telegraphed for instructions on how to stop it. After the expansion of the Hangzhou Economic Inspection Group, its focus will be on exposing large-scale hoarding. Citizens are encouraged to assist in catching the "big tigers." In addition to setting up inspection stations to prevent the outflow of materials, youth service stations and people's service stations are also being organized. Furthermore, various counties in Zhejiang are experiencing material shortages, making the regulation of inter-regional material exchange an urgent issue.

First Pacification Headquarters Orders Subordinate Areas to Organize Economic Inspection Teams 53

[Our Nantong Dispatch on the 9th] The First Pacification Headquarters has sent telegrams to all counties under its jurisdiction, ordering the organization of economic inspection teams. Their task is to inspect prices, materials, and finances. The county magistrate of each county will serve concurrently as the team leader, with representatives from the local party, government, military, and judicial departments participating, and military police will be assigned to assist in their work.

Ningbo's Supply of Goods: Chiang Ching-kuo Gives Instructions 54

Collective Purchase and Distribution by the Chamber of Commerce

[Our Yin County Dispatch on the 9th] As this area falls under the supervision of the Shanghai District, Chiang Ching-kuo is very concerned about the supply of goods, factory raw materials, and transportation enterprises in this port. Yesterday, Principal Shi of Wu Ling School visited Zhou Dalei, Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, on his way back to Feng Hua from Shanghai, conveying Chiang's instructions: (1) The supply of goods in Ningbo should be based on the Chamber of Commerce's statistics of monthly needs, with collective purchasing and distribution to various industries and markets. (2) The Xin Jiang Bridge is a vital transportation route in eastern Zhejiang, and it is hoped that local people will be motivated to raise funds quickly for its construction. After receiving the above instructions, Zhou convened representatives from various industries today to thoroughly discuss procurement methods. While acknowledging the necessity of building the Xin Jiang Bridge, the large amount of funding required necessitates further consultation with all parties to jointly plan its implementation.

Rush Buying Severe in Xiamen 55

[Our Xiamen Dispatch on the 9th] The situation of rushing to buy materials in Xiamen today has become increasingly serious. All fabric shops closed at 3 p.m., and customers crowded the entrances of stores and fabric shops. Shops that had not yet closed their doors also refused to sell. In addition to fabrics, rice shops also raised prices and refused to sell. Tonight, the municipal government convened an emergency economic meeting to discuss methods to stop this.

Wuhan Bans Export of Grain, Cloth, etc.; Price Evaluation Committee Accused of Taking Bribes 56

[Our Hankou Dispatch on the 9th] The Wuhan Municipal Government held an emergency meeting on the 9th to quell the rush to purchase goods and decided to ban the export of rice, wheat, coal, cotton yarn, cloth, and other items.

[Another Dispatch] The Wuhan Commodity Price Evaluation Committee has been accused of accepting bribes for failing to effectively evaluate and set price limits. Upon receiving the report, the Suppression Headquarters ordered the municipal government to thoroughly investigate and severely punish those involved.

Chaos in Jiangxi Market, Price Surge Breaches Economic Defenses 57

[Our Nanchang Dispatch on the 9th] The "August 19th" economic defense line in Nanchang City has been breached by price surges and the black market. Price-controlled goods such as rice, oil, and cigarettes are available only to those with money, and the grain situation is even more serious. Many citizens are filling their stomachs with noodles or glutinous rice. The provincial government is now conducting armed anti-smuggling operations on the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway South Station and Wenjiaba to prevent the export of grain. Yesterday and today, fifty large bags of rice being transported out of the area by soldiers were intercepted on the outskirts of the South Station. The Grain Bureau was ordered to purchase it at the controlled price. Edible oil is restricted to four ounces of inferior oil per person. Public sales of imported yarn are mostly monopolized by black marketeers. Prices of all kinds of goods are soaring, and the market is chaotic.

Wu Dingchang's Residence Burglarized 58

Two Thieves Caught and Sent to the Police Station for Interrogation

The police station attached great importance to the case, dispatching officers to patrol the surrounding area every night. Recently, the thieves, Li Dianchen and another, were finally apprehended and have been sent to the police station for interrogation.

My Painting Exhibition Held in New York, Gu Weijun Writes a Special Preface to Introduce It 59

[New York Air Mail] The Chinese Modern Painting Exhibition opened on the 10th at the Du Cheng Museum in New York. Dr. Gu Weijun, our ambassador to the United States, wrote a special preface to introduce it, the original text of which is as follows: "Chinese art has always occupied a unique position in the world art scene. Through the efforts of scholars and artists over several centuries, it has created a special style containing spiritual and philosophical significance. Therefore, masterpieces of all ages have been treasured by people of all countries, and their contribution to cultural exchange between Chinese and foreign people is by no means insignificant.

However, the works of modern Chinese artists are less known in various countries, which actually affects the world's understanding of modern China. In recent decades, Chinese art has made considerable progress and can fully reflect the thoughts and lives of the Chinese people today, as well as the symphony produced by contact with Western culture.

I am very willing to introduce to the American people the modern Chinese painting exhibition being actively prepared by Professors Wang Yachen and Wang Shaoling. This painting exhibition is organized by the parties concerned in cooperation with Mr. Pu Ailun of the Metropolitan Museum, who himself has extensive and profound research on Chinese culture.

Professor Wang is a famous Chinese artist and educator, who has served as the president of Xinhua Normal School for many years and was recently sent to the United States by the Ministry of Education to study art education. Mr. Wang has studied Western painting in the United States for many years and was recently hired by the Central University as a Western painting teacher.

Entrusted by the China Cultural Relics Research Association and the International Cultural Cooperation Association, Wang and Wang brought more than 120 masterpieces by famous artists for exhibition. I firmly believe that Americans who appreciate Chinese art will want to be the first to see them.

This exhibition will first be held at the Metropolitan Museum, and then will be exhibited in several other cities, so that people in all parts of the United States can have the most opportunities to directly recognize these works. I firmly believe that the noble purpose and hard work of the two gentlemen will inspire people here to develop an interested appreciation for the best modern Chinese paintings."

Truman Plans to Send Special Envoy to Moscow to Meet Stalin and Eliminate Crisis; Marshall Returns to the U.S. to Confer and Strongly Opposes; Neutral UN Representatives Mediate, But No Results Yet 63

[Reported by Our Publication] Washington, 9th (Broadcast from District): Marshall returned here this morning. President Truman had already waited at the airport and then went to the White House to hold an emergency meeting to decide whether to send a special envoy to Moscow to meet with Stalin to eliminate the differences between the U.S. and the Soviet Union, just like Hopkins' mission in 1945. It is reported that Marshall opposes this plan and advocates for its implementation to be delayed.

[Reported by Our Publication] Washington, 9th (Broadcast): Well-informed sources reported on the 9th that President Truman has appointed former Supreme Court Justice Vinson as a special envoy to Moscow to eliminate the crisis between the U.S. and the Soviet Union. The White House and the State Department have not commented on this. Secretary of State Marshall is returning to the U.S. from Paris. It is feared that Marshall's hasty return was caused by Vinson's mission to the Soviet Union. It is claimed that Marshall believes this will hinder his mission at the UN and his personal negotiations with the Soviet Union regarding the Berlin and other issues. However, according to another report, Truman consulted Marshall on this matter, and after Marshall firmly opposed it, he dismissed the idea. Therefore, Marshall's return to the U.S. is purely for the purpose of reporting directly to Truman on the international situation. Another report states that the Vinson mission was initiated and carried out by the White House and was not agreed upon by the State Department. Marshall only learned about this in Paris. It is claimed that Marshall spoke to Truman by transatlantic telephone and strongly opposed it. He will insist on opposing it to the end upon his return to the U.S.

[Associated Press, Paris, 9th] It is rumored that Truman plans to send Under Secretary of State Vinson to the Soviet Union to meet with Stalin to discuss the Berlin crisis, but Marshall strongly opposes it. The British and French delegations here are greatly puzzled by this. UN personnel believe that the attitude of the U.S. delegation has been incomprehensible in recent days. "When they first came to Paris, they were aggressive and insisted that the Berlin issue be submitted to the Security Council instead of the General Assembly. However, in recent days, their attitude has been mysterious and they have refused to disclose their purpose."

[French News Agency, Paris, 9th] The representatives of six neutral countries—China, Argentina, Colombia, Belgium, and Canada—held a private consultation this morning, chaired by Argentine Foreign Minister Bramuglia, to mediate the Berlin issue. After a seventy-minute discussion, no concrete solution was reached, and it was decided to adjourn the meeting. No date has been set for the next meeting. According to diplomatic observers, the meeting broke up without results, probably because Vyshinsky was waiting for instructions from Moscow.

Political Committee Discusses Disarmament Issue; Two Camps Engage in Verbal Sparring; Subcommittee Passes Atomic Control Plan 64

[Associated Press, Paris, 9th] The Western countries' atomic energy control plan was approved by a large majority in the UN subsidiary committee on the 9th, despite strong opposition from the Soviet Union.

[Associated Press, Paris, 9th] British representative Shawcross stated in the UN Political Committee on the 9th that the Soviet Union's current military strength is two and a half times that of before the war, and denounced the Soviet Union's disarmament proposal as "useless propaganda." Shawcross insisted that if the Soviet Union wants to reach an agreement on either disarmament or atomic control, it should be open and honest and put all its cards on the table. He also stated that unless an agreement on atomic control and measurement is reached first, there can be no agreement on the reduction of conventional armaments. Previously, Polish representative Mochnevsky launched an attack, claiming that the world's fear of war was caused by the Truman Doctrine and the Marshall Plan. He supported the proposal to reduce the military strength of the five powers by one-third within one year. Belarusian representative Kiselev repeated his old tune, accusing American personnel of planning to wage war against the Soviet Union and condemning the Western European alliance as "full of aggression."

[Our Publication] Paris, 9th (Broadcast): It is expected that the U.S. will follow Britain in rejecting the Soviet Union's proposal to reduce the military strength of the five powers by one-third within one year. The U.S. will accuse the Soviet proposal of being insincere and merely a "propaganda tactic."

Churchill Loudly Calls for No More Appeasement of the Soviet Union; Fully Supports Government's Policy on Berlin 69

[Associated Press, Ulsterton, 9th] British wartime Prime Minister Churchill said to the Conservative Party conference, "It seems that we are relentlessly moving toward the Third World War. Communist Soviet Union has fully armed, and its military strength in Europe has already exceeded the total of the Western countries." Churchill then sadly declared, "I do not want to speak empty words, but to tell you that there is still hope for reconciliation with the Soviet Union." After severely condemning "the increasingly blatant aggression and the utter betrayal of trust and justice by the Soviet government," Churchill said that he has always been confused as to why the British and American people, who have had so much experience in the past, still cannot promptly realize the danger of the Soviet Union's challenge to their lives and freedom from the East. Churchill said, "The fourteen people in the Kremlin (referring to the Soviet Politburo) arbitrarily and totalitarianly rule 300 million people, and the extent of their authority is unprecedented since Ivan the Great. They now dominate half of Europe in a communist way." Churchill said that the Berlin situation "could lead to a global war at any time." If he were in office, he would retaliate against the Soviet Union's import of war materials as a bargaining chip. He said, "The government's policy is to disregard all consequences and not retreat a single step in Berlin. We give it our full support."

The President Received Various Chiefs of This City Yesterday, Listening to Reports on Economic Management Work, Expressing Deep Appreciation for the Thorough Implementation of Economic Inspection Work; Chiang Ching-kuo Strenuously Argued That Price Controls Must Be Maintained 78

[Our Newspaper] Chiang Ching-kuo paid two successive visits to the President yesterday morning, vigorously arguing that price controls must be maintained; otherwise, the economic management work in Shanghai would inevitably be rendered futile. When Wu Kuo-chen and Wu Kai-hsien called on the President yesterday morning, they gave a detailed report on the city's control and regulation situation. Director Wu also emphasized that price controls should be coordinated with production and should not be divorced from each other; otherwise, price controls would fail. Without production, there would be no goods or prices, creating a problem of availability rather than price. After listening to the opinions separately, the President gave strict instructions on the spot. In addition, Commander Xuan also paid a visit to the President in the morning, reporting on the security situation in Shanghai.

From 3:00 PM, the President summoned Yu Hung-chun and Yu Shu-ping. The President was very concerned about the financial and price situation in Shanghai, especially the rampant speculation. After giving a detailed report, Yu Hung-chun also requested instructions on the work policy. Yu Shu-ping paid a visit at 3:30 PM. The President expressed deep appreciation for the thorough implementation of the economic inspection work in Shanghai and encouraged him to continue his efforts. He also expressed great concern for the lives of the police officers, instructing to strengthen the welfare system and pointing out that the uniforms worn by Shanghai police officers were of too poor quality, instructing Director Yu to improve them.

Further News: Supervisor Chiang Ching-kuo is scheduled to host a press conference at 6:00 PM today at the Supervisor's Office of the Central Bank to report on measures to prevent price gouging and the black market.

Economic Management Supervisor Convened Talks with the Vice Minister of Food, Discussing Ways to Smooth Grain Supply, Implementation Possible Today 79

[Our Newspaper] Economic Management Supervisor Chiang Ching-kuo convened talks with various sectors related to flour from 5:00 PM yesterday. Chen Liang, Yang Chuo'an, Rong Yiren, Cao Qidong, Sun Beiping, Zhang Chao, Feng Chunde, Yan Hongsheng, Zhong Zhigang, Yu Haixin, and others attended. Subsequently, when Vice Minister of Food Chen Liang met with reporters, he said, "Today's meeting mainly discussed how to smooth grain supply, how to strengthen and facilitate transportation, and how to enable the government and the people to cooperate closely in transporting grain. The discussions were very detailed, and considerable decisions were made. Tomorrow (referring to today), the executing agencies can proceed according to the decisions." Vice Minister Chen also stated that Shanghai's grain supply is mainly for civilian consumption, with military grain secondary, but the Ministry of Food is still trying to balance both. He believes that Shanghai's grain supply, with the cooperation of Supervisor Chiang and the relevant departments of the Ministry of Food, will definitely not be a problem.

Shanghai Flour Mills' Raw Material Inventory Dwindling Daily, Requesting the Central Government to Adjust Wheat Price Controls 80

[Our Newspaper, Nanjing, 9th] According to the Grain News Agency, Shanghai flour mills are experiencing a daily decrease in raw material inventory. Furthermore, due to the price control of 10.30 yuan, while wheat transported from Suzhou, Wuxi, and other places to Shanghai costs 11 yuan, the source has almost disappeared. Even if purchased, adulteration reaches more than 10%, greatly affecting the product. As a result, the output of various manufacturers has decreased by an average of one-half compared to the time of the August 19th price control. The Ministry of Food originally planned to purchase 1.4 million bags of flour from Shanghai factories each month, but it has had to significantly reduce this amount. Of the 700,000 bags planned for the first half of October, only 400,000 bags are guaranteed. Manufacturers have truthfully reported the impending crisis to the Ministry of Food, requesting negotiations with relevant parties to adjust the price control of wheat in Shanghai, referencing market prices in Suzhou and Wuxi, to maintain the current production situation. The Ministry of Food attaches great importance to this matter and is currently discussing a proper solution with all parties. According to the Economic Management Committee, Shanghai flour mills' request to adjust price controls has been telegraphed to the supervisor of the Shanghai region for review and handling, and a reply has been requested directly from the Ministry of Food.

Restrictions on Making Western-Style Suits: One Wool Suit Every Six Months, One Cloth Suit Every Three Months 81

Principles for Calculating Prices of Seasonal Vegetables in Vegetable Markets Determined 83

[Our Newspaper] The price controls for seasonal vegetables in vegetable markets must await approval from Director Wu of the Bureau of Social Affairs and be announced after being approved by the Price Review Committee. The principles for the Bureau of Social Affairs' review are: (1) Seasonal vegetables are priced based on the ratio of last year's rice price to this year's rice price, referencing other prices as of August 19th. (2) If there were price controls on August 19th, but adjustments are necessary due to seasonal reasons, they will also be priced based on last year's prices, referencing other prices. The price controls for other minor vegetables will not be adjusted.

Bureau of Social Affairs Invites Various Units to Discuss Prices of Tricycles and Rickshaws 84

[Our Newspaper] The Bureau of Social Affairs yesterday invited the Police Bureau, the Public Utilities Bureau, and the tricycle and rickshaw workers' union to discuss the issue of limiting price bargaining for tricycles and rickshaws. After discussion and summarization, the following opinions were reached: (1) Calculate the fare based on distance. (2) Calculate the fare based on time. (3) Establish stations at major locations, stipulating the prices between stations. Some advocated for establishing a pilot zone in busy areas to test the plan first. The Bureau of Social Affairs will convene another meeting soon for discussion and then submit it to the municipal government for approval.

Shanghai Opera Research Association Requests Higher Ticket Prices 85

[Our Newspaper] Representatives from the Shanghai Opera Research Association, accompanied by Senator Zhang Zhongyuan, went to the Bureau of Social Affairs yesterday, claiming that the ticket prices for Shanghai opera theaters in the city are too low, and staff cannot maintain their livelihoods, requesting higher ticket prices. The Bureau of Social Affairs instructed them to maintain the original prices, and the proposed adjustment of ticket prices will be submitted to the Price Review Committee for discussion.

Fifteen Merchants Detained and Punished for Black Market Transactions in Teahouses 86

[Our Newspaper] Yesterday, the Economic Police Brigade captured merchants Wang Jia-zhi, Tao Wen-pei, Xu Zhong-lin, Lou Xin, Zhou Bin-ying, Zhang Ji-qiang, Fang Xi-qi, Zhou Si-he, Wang Zhao-fu, Zhang Chuan-gui, and others, totaling fifteen, who were engaged in black market transactions involving cotton cloth, wool, oilcloth, and canned goods in the Qinglian Pavilion and Changle teahouses on Fuzhou Road. After being taken to the bureau for interrogation, they were punished according to the severity of their offenses under the Police Violation Regulations.

Ma Jingxiu Prosecuted for Stockpiling Soap

[Our Newspaper] Zhang Siwei, manager of Xinji Motor Oil Company, and Wu Guoliang, manager of New York Motor Oil Company, Zhang Xin-hai, stockpiled more than 500 barrels of motor oil, which had not been sold for more than two months. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's New Ship Haiwen Arrives in Shanghai 90

[Our Newspaper] China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's new ship Haiwen arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning and is currently docked at the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's pier. The ship was purchased on behalf of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company by Huashang Steamship Company in Singapore. Originally named S.S. Montoro, it was originally an Australian ship. It has a gross tonnage of 4,057 tons, is 360 feet 6 inches long, 47 feet 2 inches wide, and has a horsepower of 661. It has three boilers (coal-fired), a speed of 12 knots per hour, and luxurious and comfortable passenger accommodations. First class can accommodate 170 people, third class 200 people, and fourth class 400 people. There is no second class. The cargo hold also has air conditioning equipment and can load 40 tons of fresh goods. After some minor repairs, it will operate on the Shanghai-Keelung line and the Nanyang line.

A Large Quantity of Smuggled Saccharin Found Hidden on the Ship California 91

Yesterday, when the ship California arrived in Shanghai from Guam, an American engineer named Jessie occupied a cabin and an empty room on the ship. Jianghai Customs anti-smuggling personnel boarded the ship for inspection and found compartments in the two rooms. After searching, they discovered a total of eighty-one boxes and seventy-four bags of smuggled saccharin. After interrogation, the engineer confessed that he owned it and had hidden it in the compartments. In addition to the customs handling the smuggled goods according to the anti-smuggling regulations, the engineer Jessie was transferred to the District Attorney's Office for investigation in accordance with the Regulations on Punishing Smuggling.

Twelve Organizations Including the Municipal Council Form a Price Negotiation Committee, Responsible for Reviewing Prices of Non-Essential Daily Necessities 92

[Our Newspaper] The Municipal Government will soon organize a Price Negotiation Committee in accordance with the Supplementary Regulations of the New Economic Policy of the Executive Yuan. In the future, in addition to the prices of important commodities being reviewed by the Shanghai District Price Review Committee, the Price Negotiation Committee will be responsible for preliminary review of prices of other non-essential daily necessities that need to be adjusted, and then the Price Review Committee will discuss them. The Price Negotiation Committee will be composed of representatives from twelve units, including the Municipal Government, the Municipal Council, the Police Bureau, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Industrial Association, the General Labor Union, the China Trust Bureau, the Public Utilities Bureau, the Health Bureau, the Local Court, the Materials Supply Bureau, and the Bureau of Social Affairs, and will be convened by the Bureau of Social Affairs. It is also learned that the first meeting of the committee will be held within the week. The spokesman for the Economic Management Supervisor's Office stated yesterday that no prices are allowed to be adjusted arbitrarily without the approval of the Price Review Committee. The price increase of woolen yarn this time was not approved by the Price Review Committee in advance, which is clearly unreasonable, and the police bureau has been ordered to carry out a crackdown.

Wool Yarn Shops Temporarily Close, Price Issue Pending Review 93

Before the price is approved, manufacturers cannot open, and the Bureau of Social Affairs has ordered the woolen yarn industry to temporarily close its business and wait for the approved price.

Li Xingji Suspected of Stockpiling Sugar, Fifteen Sets of Forged Account Books Confiscated 94

Special Criminal Court Convenes Meeting Regarding Suspected Student Cases 95

Xu Shixian, chief prosecutor of the Special Criminal Court, and prosecutors Zhu Cheng, Mao Jihe, Li Yulong, and Wang Nai Zhang who were in charge of the case all attended. After this meeting, the defendants who will be indicted and those who will not be indicted can be determined within a few days.

Shipowners' Association General Meeting Successfully Concluded Yesterday Afternoon 96

A Total of Seventy-Nine Matters Discussed

The General Materials Inspection Concluded, Chief Commander Yu Recommended to the Economic Supervisor That Warehouses Be Ordered to Create Lists for Verification 97

[Our Newspaper] The city's general materials inspection continued yesterday and was completed as scheduled by the evening. The types of materials, locations, and names of owners in each district where the inspected quantities did not match the registered quantities or were moved without authorization are being sorted out by each police precinct and are expected to be submitted to the General Headquarters for review and handling next Monday. Mr. Yu Shuping met with reporters at 6:00 PM yesterday and said: "This general materials inspection was successfully completed with the assistance of all parties, which is very gratifying. During the inspection process, it was found that many manufacturers' materials were stored in several districts. In other words, the warehouses in a certain area often stored materials from manufacturers in other areas, and some merchants moved the materials without authorization after registration, which made verification very difficult during the inspection." He has recommended to the Economic Supervisor's Office to order the warehouse industry association to notify all warehouses to quickly list in detail the types, quantities, periods, and owners of the materials stored as of the 8th of this month and submit them to the Bureau of Social Affairs for comparison with the results of the general inspection. Those who conceal and fail to report will be treated as underground warehouses and severely punished.

It is learned that the two subcommittees of the council, the Police Administration and Regulations Subcommittees, convened separate meetings yesterday, re-elected the conveners, and then convened a joint meeting of the two subcommittees to discuss this issue specifically. However, it is learned that the precise research at that time focused on the organizational issues of the garrison brigade, and no concrete conclusions were reached yesterday regarding the large amount of funds required for the brigade's establishment and the maintenance costs after its establishment.

The Coal Adjustment Office Was Ordered to Close and Hand Over to the Mining and Commercial Association 99

A Large-Scale Health Exhibition Will Be Held Today at Aurora University, with an Electric Lung Disease Model that Is Most Thought-Provoking 100

[Our Newspaper] The Municipal Health Bureau, in view of the excessively high morbidity and mortality rates of Shanghai citizens, and in order to make the general public aware of the importance of hygiene and medicine in a popular way, has specially organized a large-scale health exhibition, which will be open to the public free of charge at the auditorium of Aurora University starting from Double Ten Festival. This kind of exhibition is still a pioneering event in the city after the victory. The preparatory work is jointly undertaken by the Bureaus of Education, Public Utilities, and Public Works, as well as more than ten organizations including Tongji, Aurora, St. John's, Tongde, Shanghai, and Southeast Medical Colleges, Shanghai Dental College, Pasteur Institute, Anti-Tuberculosis Association, and the United States Information Service. The exhibits include fifteen groups such as decomposition and anatomy, physiology, pathology, bacteria, parasites, infectious disease management, nursing, maternal and child health, school hygiene, and factory hygiene. The order of display is: the first part explains the structure of the human body, the second part explains the sources of disease, and the third part explains how to improve health. Each exhibition room has eye-catching slogans and statistical charts attached to the walls. Among them, the lung disease exhibition room is equipped with a thunderous model, with a sickbed on the left and a coffin on the right. The explanation in the middle states that only 3.1 million people died in the war of resistance against Japan in the past eight years, but as many as 10.8 million people died of lung disease. On average, 3 million out of every 100,000 people die of lung disease each year. In terms of wealth loss, if each lung disease patient spends one gold yuan per day, society must spend 5 billion gold yuan each year in addition to not being able to increase production. This model is novel and most thought-provoking.

Part of the Health Exhibition Hall (Photo by This Newspaper)

Daily Necessities Difficult to Purchase as Required, The General Labor Union Registers and Asks the Authorities to Implement Rationing 102

Since the government promulgated the Emergency Financial and Economic Measures on August 19 this year, issued gold yuan, and implemented currency reform, national prices have been limited to the August 19 prices, and the index-based salary calculation method has been abolished, so workers' wages have also been frozen. The gold yuan conversion standard is calculated based on the cost of living index announced on August 15. The Municipal General Labor Union believes that the index is based on the average prices from August 1 to August 13, which is far from the price limits on August 19, and some workers have not yet been able to convert into gold yuan according to the index, so it is believed that the losses suffered by workers are quite large. In particular, in recent days, it has been difficult for workers to purchase daily necessities at the limited prices, so the union has repeatedly reported the hardships of workers to the government authorities and requested appropriate adjustments, but due to the current economic management situation, the request has not been approved, so the lives of general workers have been greatly threatened. After the union submitted it to the 53rd council meeting for discussion, it was decided to register all union members and their families in the city, so as to request the government to implement rationing at limited prices to maintain the inadequacy of life. After careful consideration by the responsible persons of the union, the resolution was notified to all industry unions in the city yesterday to comply with and organize an investigation committee.

Twenty-Five Units Have Purchased Enemy and Puppet Properties 103

As of yesterday, there were 25 units in the China Trust Bureau that had priority to purchase enemy and puppet properties. The China Trust Bureau issued the notification letters in four batches. Currently, the purchasers are all those who received the first batch of letters, so the priority purchase situation is very optimistic. The deadline for the first batch of China Trust Bureau's priority purchase of enemy and puppet properties is set to begin on the 15th of this month.

A Soldier Who Was Dismissed Had Evil Intentions and Abused the Daughter of the Uniform Shop Owner, Forcing Her to Leave Her Family and Sending Her to the District Attorney's Office for Questioning 104

[Our Newspaper] Dai Hongxin, owner of the Dai Hongji uniform shop at No. 757, Jiujiang Road, has a daughter named Bingxia, who is twenty-one years old and beautiful. Dai loves her like a pearl. Zhou Keding, 25, a former soldier of the 23rd Regiment of the Military Police stationed in the 3rd Brigade of the Garrison Headquarters, was dismissed due to misconduct. He came to the shop to have a uniform made and gradually became intimate with the daughter. Zhou, with evil intentions, was determined to force himself on Bingxia, and Hongxin asked about his military status. In early December of last year, Dai returned to his hometown with his family, leaving his daughter in charge of the store. Zhou learned of this situation and sneaked into the daughter's room one night and forced himself on her. The daughter was unable to resist and was abused. At about 11:00 PM on the 7th of this month, Zhou came to the store again and insisted on inviting the daughter out to talk. The daughter refused, and Zhou became angry and wrote a threatening letter, ordering Dai to hand it over to his daughter. The next morning, the daughter received a call from Zhou, asking her to meet at the Nanguo Restaurant, otherwise he would deal with her severely. The daughter was in a dilemma and finally went to the meeting. She then went to Zhou's residence at No. 27, Guizhou Road, and Zhou took out a sharp blade, forcing the daughter to leave her family and marry him. The daughter pretended to go home, and Zhou followed her to the store. When he saw the daughter's father, he slapped him twice and threatened him. Someone called the police, who arrived and took Zhou to the bureau for interrogation and confirmed the facts. Zhou was accused of obstructing family and transferred to the District Attorney's Office for investigation.

Liu Yuqing Defends Against Bank Law Violation Charges with Four Points 105

[Report from our newspaper] Liu Yuqing, a businessman newly arrived in Shanghai from Peiping and Tianjin, residing at Cishu Mansion, was previously accused of using the Tianjin Yixing Factory Office as a cover to continuously engage in private banking operations since May of this year. After police investigation, codebooks and telegrams were seized on the spot, and it was determined that the amount of funds transferred from Tianjin reached a substantial sum of 6,000 Gold Yuan. The case was transferred to the District Procuratorate for investigation and closure, and Liu was prosecuted for violating banking laws. The District Court held a hearing yesterday afternoon, where Liu, accompanied by his lawyer, presented four points in his defense: (1) The 6,000 Gold Yuan remittance was borrowed from the Dalu Bank of Tai City for the purpose of purchasing cotton yarn in Shanghai, as evidenced by the loan agreement from Dalu Bank; it was not a foreign exchange speculation. (2) The seized drafts of letters concerned the severe economic controls in Shanghai after "August 19th" [referring to the currency reform of August 19, 1948], and contained nothing else. (3) The secret code was used by the former residents of the office, Xinyi and Fuqian, for foreign exchange speculation, and the defendant himself did not understand it. (4) The destroyed documents were mere notes and not important documents. After the defense, the court briefly questioned the points provided and scheduled the verdict for the afternoon of the sixteenth.

Street Lights Near Tian Yao Bridge Road Installed and Lit 106

[Report from our newspaper] The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities recently installed six street lights at Qu'an and Wangjiatang near Tian Yao Bridge Road in western Shanghai. All lights have been turned on. These two locations are important thoroughfares connecting Jinji Bridge and Xie Tu Road. Yang Anren et al.'s Request for Retrial Rejected Again by the District Court 107

[Report from our newspaper] The Jinchao case, which has attracted nationwide attention, was previously heard by Judge Wang Jiazhuo of the District Court. Yang Anren was sentenced to seven years of imprisonment, and Mo Sheng was sentenced to four years of imprisonment. The defendants applied for a retrial, but the High Court determined that the original judgment was appropriate in both the application of the law and the sentencing, and approved the original judgment, transferring them to the Shanghai Prison. Subsequently, Yang and others, citing new evidence, applied for a retrial, which was repeatedly rejected by the District Court in accordance with the law. Recently, the High Court, based on an appeal, remanded the case for a new ruling. For the sake of prudence, the District Court telegraphed the Supreme Court to transfer the case to the Capital District Court or another court for handling. The Supreme Court reviewed the case file and determined that the case did not need to be transferred, replying that it could still be handled impartially by the Shanghai District Court. Having learned this, the District Court believed that Yang and others' application for a retrial was still without legal basis and rejected it in a ruling yesterday. The ruling was immediately served to all parties involved.

Fire on Huashan Road Destroys Candle Shop 108

Also Affects Neighboring Ham Shop and Foil Shop

[Report from our newspaper] The Gangan Candle Shop at 2080 Huashan Road in western Shanghai caught fire at approximately 3:26 PM yesterday due to careless cooking. Because the materials stored inside were all oil-based, once ignited, fierce flames erupted, making it impossible to approach. In an instant, the entire shop was destroyed. The fire also affected the neighboring Faxing Ham Shop at 2082, burning away half of it, and the roof of the Shenghe Foil Shop at 2084. Fire brigades from the Huashan Road and Yuyuan Road fire districts, as well as the Central Fire Department, rushed to the scene and extinguished the fire at around 6 PM. Fortunately, there were no casualties, but the damage was significant. The person responsible for the fire was taken into custody by the local police precinct for investigation and handling.

Suzhou Authorities Seize Shanghai Merchant's Hoarded Paper Stored for Five Years 111

[Report from our Suzhou, 9th] The Suzhou City Defense Command recently seized 40 rolls of newsprint in the warehouse of the Yifengshen Paper Shop on Wannianqiao Street outside the Xumen Gate and brought the shop's accountant, Wu Qichang, to the county government for handling. The military law office of the county government has now concluded its investigation. It was determined that the white newsprint was purchased and stored by Wang Meifang, manager of the Hongfengxin Paper Shop on Chongqing Road in Shanghai, in 1943 and has been stored for five years. This is clearly hoarding with the intention of making excessive profits and should be confiscated in accordance with the regulations on cracking down on hoarding of important daily necessities. The case has been transferred to the court for adjudication, and orders have been issued to arrest Wang Meifang and Yao Zhang, manager of the Yifengshen Paper Shop, to be brought to justice.

As a result of petitions from the National Money Industry Association, the requirement to pay in one lump sum was allowed. On the 9th, installment payments were approved. Banks are required to pay 5,000 Gold Yuan before the completion of capital increase, and money shops are required to pay 2,500 Gold Yuan before the completion of capital increase.

Promoting Production of State-Owned Enterprises: Issuance of Corporate Bonds to be Approved; Pilot Program to Begin with Factories and Mines Affiliated with the Resources Commission 116

[Report from our newspaper] According to authoritative sources in the financial community, in order to facilitate state-owned enterprises in obtaining working capital needed for production without increasing currency issuance, the government will allow the issuance of corporate bonds to guide social idle funds through banking organizations for use in production. The plan is to start with a pilot program involving factories and mines affiliated with the Resources Commission, with national banks and bureaus underwriting the bonds and then reselling them to the public. Detailed measures are being discussed and drafted by the Central Bank and various national banks and bureaus. According to relevant sources, the issuance of corporate bonds is not only easier to raise funds, but also simpler in terms of repayment procedures. The public can purchase these bonds, which are stable and reliable with regular repayment and a certain amount of interest. In recent years, the issuance of corporate bonds has been highly developed in Europe and the United States and is an effective way to use private funds. Once the pilot program for state-owned enterprises proves successful, private enterprises may also follow suit.

Cotton Yarn Needed in the Market Supplied Through Allocation by National Banks: China Textile Construction Corporation Held Third Board Meeting Yesterday 117

[Report from our newspaper] The China Textile Construction Corporation (紡建) held its third board meeting at 3:30 PM yesterday, chaired by Chen Qitian. The following resolutions were made as a result of the discussions:

(1) After 紡建 is reorganized into a joint-stock company, all personnel, administrative, and business management methods will be handled in accordance with general company practices, and past systems will be adjusted accordingly.

(2) 紡建's current yarn inventory is only sufficient to repay the 行總 (Executive Yuan War Relief Supplies Bureau), the Textile Export Association, and US Aid cotton yarn, with no remaining amount available for the market. Future market supply issues will be managed by the Central Bank through yarn allocation.

(3) The current General Manager Shu Yunzhang is firm in his intention to resign. However, he will remain in his position in the short term until the board of directors can find a suitable replacement.

(4) Li Bingyu was appointed to represent 紡建 at the World Textile Industry Conference to be held in Geneva.

Cotton Yarn and Cloth Production Declines Daily 118

The problem of raw materials has not been resolved, and as a result of panic buying, cotton yarn and cloth production has declined, and factories are reducing production. Pan Shihao, chairman of the 复织 Association (Re-weaving Association), suggested that a portion of the 60,000 bales of 行總 (Executive Yuan War Relief Supplies Bureau) cotton yarn stored in the Central Bank be allocated to the market to meet the urgent needs. However, due to the inability to resolve foreign exchange issues, the dyestuffs required by the re-weaving industry have become limited in stock recently and difficult to replenish. Although they can be purchased on the black market, the prices are twice as high as the controlled prices, which will increase costs. Purchasing from the black market would violate the law. Therefore, the industry hopes that the authorities will quickly resolve the raw material problem. Furthermore, the factories of the Qingdao China Textile Branch Company have recently felt a severe shortage of raw materials and are requesting the headquarters to quickly find a way to allocate a large amount of cotton to meet their urgent needs. The company is currently writing to the Cotton Group to quickly allocate the second batch of aid cotton.

Furthermore, according to reports, the yarn market continues to be closed. Small-scale handicrafts manufacturers in the city, for whom cotton yarn is the main raw material, and wholesalers from Suzhou and Hangzhou, have come to Shanghai to compete for purchases from yarn shops, causing Jinling Road yarn wholesale shops to be very crowded. Buyers are mainly interested in the four types of yarn with counts of 16, 20, 32, and 40.

Dull Silk Market 119

The rayon market remains sluggish. The allocation by the association did not reach its quota yesterday. Japanese goods are no longer available in the market. The raw materials of the Italian goods miscellaneous silk fabrics are considered too substandard, and applications for allocation have decreased. Raw silk transactions are quiet. Sellers are unwilling to sell, and buyers are not interested due to the lack of foreign transportation. The silk weaving industry on this street is mostly applying to the 輸管會 (Export Control Board) for allocation, and only sporadic transactions are taking place in the market.

Retail sales of silk fabrics have begun to slacken. Sichuan silk is becoming scarce due to restrictions on out-of-province sales. Silk factories are about to begin allocating goods, which has somewhat stabilized people's minds.

Furthermore, according to reports, the Central Trust Bureau, acting as an agent for the Government Property Disposal Committee, distributed over 400 boxes of rayon this week and sold woolens, sundries, etc. at auction, obtaining a total of 1.4 million Gold Yuan. It is scheduled to auction off sundries and other goods next Friday.

China Textile Corporation Sells Cloth 120

Since the cotton cloth market has been suspended, the business of wholesale firms has suddenly declined due to transportation restrictions. Retail cloth shops, stimulated by the panic buying, have sold out their inventories, and their replenishment relies on the supply of cloth from the building weaving industry and the China Textile Construction Corporation. The supply source is still considered sufficient. It is reported that the染织业 (dyeing and weaving industry) has entrusted the Cotton Cloth Association to distribute the first batch of 35,000 pieces, of which a total of 12,000 pieces have been distributed.

The second batch of 64,000 pieces, due to the wide variety of patterns, coincided with the surge in panic buying, and cloth shops were eager to replenish their inventories, so the allocation quota is almost exhausted, with only a few hundred pieces remaining. It is reported that a third batch of 60,000 pieces will be allocated next Monday, with the association preparing to distribute 20,000 pieces first. The China Textile Corporation continues to distribute cloth every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday as usual, but due to the surge in demand, the number of customers allocated has been slightly limited. Yesterday, 9-pound 3B Longtou fine cloth was distributed at a price of 18.6 yuan. This fine cloth was originally manufactured for export, with a width of 36 inches and a length of only 30 yards.

Central Bank Changes Regulations on Security Deposits for Silver and Money Industries 121

According to a spokesperson for the Central Bank, President Yu has revised the regulations regarding the request from the money industry to be exempt from paying security deposits for clearing: (1) Pay half of the prescribed amounts of 10,000, 5,000, and 3,000. (2) Half of the reduced security deposit must be paid before the 10th of this month, and the remaining half must be paid after the completion of the capital increase. Banks must pay the security deposit as prescribed. Half must be paid before October 10th, and the other half must be paid after the capital increase is completed. The Central Bank has notified the banking and money industries in various regions to comply with the above measures.

Furthermore, it has been learned that the request from the banking and money industries to reduce the amount of capital increase is impossible.

Ministry of Finance Reinterprets Bank Loan-to-Deposit Ratio 122

[Report from our newspaper] Regarding how to calculate the percentage of credit loans, real estate mortgage loans, or investments to the total amount of deposits as stipulated in the Banking Law, the Ministry of Finance previously stipulated that the total amount of deposits should be calculated on a consolidated basis for the entire bank. It is now learned that, for the sake of calculation convenience, the Ministry of Finance has further clarified in detail as follows: The percentage of such loans and investments to the total amount of deposits "can be calculated by adding and subtracting interbank transactions (adding credit balance and subtracting debit balance) to the deposits of each head office and branch office, resulting in the individual deposits of each head office and branch office, and then calculating the percentage with its individual credit loans, real estate mortgage loans, or investments, in order to simplify the process. If funds other than deposits are used for various loans or investments, they should be included in the calculation of deposits."

Export Control Board Announces Export Prices for Export Goods 123

[Report from our newspaper] The minimum export prices for export goods announced by the Export Control Board in its eighth announcement were generally the same as last week, but some prices have changed slightly, as follows:

Bristles (black), Hankou No. 17 blended bristles, US$4.50 per pound (increased by US$0.25 compared to last week); down feathers (Nanjing, Wuhu, Shanghai, containing 18% down), US$0.31 per pound (decreased by US$0.02 compared to last week); duck feathers (Hankou, containing 14-15% down), US$0.28 per pound (decreased by US$0.02 compared to last week); duck feathers (Sichuan, containing 12% down), US$0.25 per pound (decreased by US$0.02 compared to last week).

Export Consignment Goods: Overdue Exchange Settlement Calculated at 70% 125

[Report from our newspaper] The National Bank Business Bureau recently sent Circular No. 158 to various designated banks, stating: "Regarding the measures for overdue exchange settlement of export consignment goods, as stipulated in this bank's Circular Nos. 134 and 154, we hereby amend that, from today onwards, all overdue exchange settlement of export consignment goods shall be calculated at 70% of the current exchange rate. The provisions of Section 5 of this bank's former Circular No. 134 and Circular No. 154 shall be immediately repealed."

Sluggish Rice Market; Grain Transactions Enter a State of Stagnation 126

Rice continues to arrive, but there are very few transactions in the market. The North Market has 502 shi of Bai Geng and Yang Xian rice, and the South Market has 313 shi, for a total of 815 shi. There are also rice shops selling 110 shi of rice on their own. Although the above rice is sold at controlled prices, it can only be purchased by those who are close to the owners, so transactions have not yet returned to normal.

Grain transactions have almost entered a state of stagnation. Only dozens of bags of raw peanuts were officially offered in the city. Soybeans are difficult to buy, and there are no transactions for corn, red beans, or broad beans. No one is selling high-quality sesame seeds, and no one is buying low-quality sesame seeds, so no transactions have taken place. Kaifeng raw peanuts are 32.7 yuan, and new 生　 are 35.7 yuan.

Active Tea Market 127

Yesterday, the foreign firm tea market was relatively active. Because exporters feel that the demand for tea in Europe and Africa is strong, buying interest remains high. However, holders of goods feel that the production season has passed and the market inventory is very scarce, so they remain hesitant, resulting in few attractive transactions. The potential profit is unparalleled.

It is reported that a certain company in the city has received a telegram from Morocco requesting an immediate shipment of 50 tons of 屯 Green tea to meet urgent needs. However, under the above circumstances, the person in charge of the company is currently unable to respond. As for domestic sales tea, there is also a shortage of supply and an excess of demand, and the market atmosphere is firm in the quiet.

Sugar Still Popular 128

The sugar market was popular again yesterday. The prices of various grades are close to the limit. Because the sugar industry will implement an allocation system and stop market transactions, it is generally expected that the supply will be limited, so those in need are taking the opportunity to buy in advance. The amount of goods in the market suddenly decreased, and people's minds became firmer, with most holders watching the situation. No. 22 sand white, No. 45 car white精 sugar are not available in the market, and no prices have been quoted. Medium sand, Xinghua white, Gao Ben factory cotton white are mostly in demand, while the rest are consistent.

High Prices for Bricks, Ashes, and Other Goods 129

The shortage of bricks and ashes is becoming more serious, and builders, unable to stop construction on half-completed houses, are collecting them regardless of the high prices, making the atmosphere of overpricing even more intense. Since the factory stopped supplying cement, retailers have been unable to supply large quantities, and it is difficult to purchase even ten or twenty bags. Realizing Reality and Engaging in Construction Research: Joint Annual Meeting of Scientific Organizations: Ren Hongjun Speaks on: The Scientist at the Crossroads: Opened in Beijing Yesterday Morning for Three Days 130

[Report from our Nanjing, 9th] The 37th Joint Annual Meeting of ten scientific organizations, including the China Society for Natural Sciences, the Science Society of China, the New China Mathematical Society, the Chinese Astronomical Society, the Chinese Physical Society, the Chinese Geophysical Society, the Chinese Geographical Society, the Chinese Meteorological Society, the Chinese Zoological Society, and the Chinese Genetics Society, opened in Beijing on the morning of the 9th.

Opening Ceremony

The opening ceremony was held at the Central University Auditorium at 9:00 AM, chaired by Zhou Hongjing. Guests present included Weng Wenhao, Zhou Yichun, Chen Qitian (represented by Wu Chengluo), Shi Fade (representative of the联教组织驻华代表), and many members. The chairman announced the opening of the meeting and briefly reported on the significance of the meeting. Then, Dean Weng, in his capacity as honorary president, delivered a speech, stating that science progresses through research, regardless of current human thought. However, communism seeks to control human thought and unify the world with political power. Therefore, the共匪 do not hesitate to create social instability through armed rebellion, let alone consider the impact on scientific research. Under such circumstances, political awakening can enable the promotion of science. Today's scientists should realize reality, review the old and learn the new, and strive to engage in constructive research. Subsequently, Chairman Zhu Jiahua delivered a speech, pointing out that the biggest difficulty in current scientific research is the issue of funding. Although the efforts of the academic community have not stopped in the past ten years, the Academia Sinica has established a perfect research system in 20 years. He encouraged all groups to cooperate and overcome material difficulties to improve academic standards. Vice President Shen Yi said that in the politically charged capital, the holding of the Joint Annual Meeting is a voice from the desert. The holding of a grand exhibition is thanked on behalf of all citizens and wishes to share "Do not speak, we continue to work in disappointment" with scientists and engineers. Then, Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, representing Wu Chengluo, President Gu Yuxiu of National Chengchi University, Director Selo of the British Council Science Group, and others delivered speeches one after another, comforting the hard work of research and expecting greater success. Finally, Shen Qiyi, Secretary-General of the Organizing Committee, reported on the preparation process, and then Ren Hongjun gave the annual meeting speech. The topic was "The Scientist at the Crossroads." The photography ceremony was completed at about 12:00 noon.

Annual Meeting Schedule

The annual meeting is scheduled for three days. On the afternoon of the 9th, there will be a special discussion on "How to Promote the Development of Science in Our Country." The joint association affairs will also be discussed. On the morning of the 10th, the Capital Science Exhibition will open, and papers will be read in groups. In the afternoon, the affairs of various academic societies will be discussed. On the morning of the 11th, papers will be read in groups by various academic societies. In the afternoon, a collective visit will be made to the Capital Science Exhibition. The annual meeting will then be declared closed.

Spicing Up the National Day Holiday: Fuxing Cup Final Today, China National Aviation Corporation vs. Samsung at 3:00 PM 141

In the Fuxing Cup Small Football Tournament held at the city stadium, China National Aviation Corporation (CNAC) defeated the strong Huidar 4-2 in overtime in yesterday's semi-final, while Samsung defeated the lively Longtou 1-0, securing their places in the final. They will compete for the overall championship today on the National Day holiday.

The skills of the players in the Huidar-CNAC match were very evenly matched. In the first half, CNAC's Yu Zhenyue scored a penalty kick. In the second half, Huidar's Gu Qingbing also tied the score with a nine-meter penalty kick. Gu then scored another goal, putting Huidar ahead 2-1. In the end, CNAC got another nine-meter penalty kick opportunity, and Yu Zhenyue scored, making it 2-2. Since the score was tied at the end of regulation time, there was a twenty-minute overtime. CNAC's Yu Musen and Jin Jiabiao each scored a goal, giving them the final victory with a score of 4-2. Although Huidar lost, their strength was no less than that of CNAC. The referee was Xu Guoliang.

In the second match between Samsung and Longtou, both sides played very cleanly and admirably. After more than ten minutes of stalemate, Samsung advanced on the left side, Xiao Ziwen crossed the ball, and Lin Dianyi shot it in, opening the scoring and securing the victory with this solitary goal. In the second half, Longtou counterattacked, and their offensive became even more intense in the last five minutes. Samsung's Lu Zhengxiang committed a handball in the penalty area, and Yao Qingsheng took a penalty kick. Longtou's failure to score sealed their fate. The result was still 1-0. The referee was Ma Youyu.

Samsung and CNAC are scheduled to hold the final match for the overall championship at 3:00 pm today. The referee is Fang Rongfu, and the linesmen are Zang Wenbin and Xu Guoliang.
